# Test source

```ts
  11  | const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
  12  | 
  13  | const BASE_URL = 'https://nxthire.ai';
  14  | const CREDS = {
  15  |   email:    process.env.NXTHIRE_EMAIL,
  16  |   password: process.env.NXTHIRE_PASSWORD,
  17  | };
  18  | 
  19  | // ── Login helper ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  20  | async function login(page) {
  21  |   await page.goto(`${BASE_URL}/login`, { timeout: 60000 });
  22  |   await page.fill('input[type="email"]',    CREDS.email);
  23  |   await page.fill('input[type="password"]', CREDS.password);
  24  |   await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
  25  |   await page.waitForURL('**/dashboard', { timeout: 60000 });
  26  | }
  27  | 
  28  | // ── Navigate to Open Jobs page ────────────────────────────────
  29  | async function goToJobs(page) {
  30  |   await page.goto(`${BASE_URL}/jobs`, { timeout: 60000 });
  31  |   await page.waitForTimeout(4000);
  32  | }
  33  | 
  34  | // ── Get page body text ────────────────────────────────────────
  35  | async function getBody(page) {
  36  |   return await page.locator('body').innerText().catch(() => '');
  37  | }
  38  | 
  39  | // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  70  |   });
  71  |

  80  |     expect(hasActiveReqs).toBe(true);

      |                           ^ Error: expect(received).toBe(expected) // Object.is equality

  115 |   test('Source filter has Ceipal option', async ({ page }) => {
  116 |     // Source filter is a native select element
  117 |     const select = page.locator('select').first();
  118 |     const visible = await select.isVisible().catch(() => false);
  119 |     if (visible) {
  120 |       const options = await select.locator('option').allInnerTexts();
  121 |       console.log(`Source filter options: ${options.join(', ')}`);
  122 |       const hasCeipal = options.some(o => o.toLowerCase().includes('ceipal'));
  123 |       console.log(`Ceipal option present: ${hasCeipal}`);
  124 |       expect(hasCeipal).toBe(true);
  125 |       console.log('PASS: Ceipal option in source filter');
  126 |     } else {
  127 |       // Try reading options from body text
  128 |       const body = await getBody(page);
  129 |       const hasCeipal = body.includes('Ceipal');
  130 |       console.log(`Ceipal found in page: ${hasCeipal}`);
  131 |       expect(hasCeipal).toBe(true);
  132 |     }
  133 |   });
  134 | 
  135 |   test('Selecting Ceipal filters jobs correctly', async ({ page }) => {
  136 |     const select = page.locator('select').first();
  137 |     const visible = await select.isVisible().catch(() => false);
  138 |     if (visible) {
  139 |       const options = await select.locator('option').allInnerTexts();
  140 |       const ceipalOption = options.find(o => o.toLowerCase().includes('ceipal'));
  141 |       if (ceipalOption) {
  142 |         await select.selectOption({ label: ceipalOption });
  143 |         await page.waitForTimeout(3000);
  144 |         const body = await getBody(page);
  145 |         const hasReqs = body.includes('requisitions') || body.includes('loaded');
  146 |         console.log(`After Ceipal filter — reqs visible: ${hasReqs}`);
  147 |         console.log('PASS: Ceipal filter applied');
  148 |       }
  149 |     } else {
  150 |       console.log('NOTE: Source filter is a custom component — manual verification needed');
  151 |     }
  152 |   });
  153 | 
  154 | });
```
